**High probability:** A period of conspicuous *under-deployment* immediately following the loss of Krakoan infrastructure. He will rationalize this in tactical terms ("we need to keep a low profile," "civilians are watching") but the underlying mechanism will be the old one — permission withdrawn, throttle re-engaged. Expect a 6–12 month window in which his combat output drops noticeably below his Krakoan baseline.

**Moderate probability:** A *single* high-stakes crisis within that window will force a brief return to Omega expression. The crisis-shape that historically pulls full output from him involves (a) a threat to Hank McCoy or to a younger mutant under his informal mentorship, or (b) a mass-casualty scenario in which civilian death is imminent and no other mutant present can prevent it. When the trigger fires, output will be disproportionate, will frighten observers, and — critical fork — will either be metabolized ("I can do this and the world did not end") or rapidly re-suppressed ("I scared myself, I scared them, never again"). The pattern record favors re-suppression by roughly 4:1, but the post-Krakoan baseline shifts the ratio meaningfully toward integration.

**Low probability but worth flagging:** Catastrophic over-expression. He has never lost control in the volatility sense — the escalation curve goes into *capacity*, not chaos. But the somatic-dissociative pathway remains open, and a sufficiently acute combination of grief + permission-collapse + isolation could produce a *refusal to revert* event of long duration. The 1990s arc of being stuck in ice-form is the template; the post-Mystique shattering is the more dangerous variant. A multi-week or multi-month ice-form withdrawal under sufficient stress is plausible and would be functionally a dissociative fugue with somatic expression.

### 2.2 Romantic and intimate life

The Krakoan-era partnership(s) established a new floor. The likely pattern over the next 18–36 months is **serial short-to-medium-term relationships of improving quality.** He is unlikely to land in a durable long-term partnership immediately; the avoidant defense is still operational and intimacy past the six-to-eighteen month mark remains the historical break point. Expect:

- Continued preference for partners who share the mutant/super context (the closet-residue: he is still safer with partners who do not require concealment).
- Continued sub-pattern of choosing partners who are in some way *in transit* — geographically, professionally, or developmentally — which permits the relationship to end without the rupture feeling like rejection. Romeo of the Inhumans is the template; expect variations.
- A meaningful probability (perhaps 35–45%) that within this window he attempts and aborts at least one cohabitation. The aborted cohabitation will be presented as logistical; it will be attachment.

The fork point in this domain is whether he forms one durable attachment that *survives* his attempt to sabotage it. He has never had this. If it occurs — if a partner refuses to be pushed away on schedule — the trajectory shifts substantially.

### 2.3 Family of origin

William Drake is, on the publication timeline, an elderly man. The forward window includes, with high probability, **his father's death.** This is the single most consequential pending event in Bobby's near-term emotional life and the file should treat it as such.

Three sub-trajectories present:

- **The reconciliation case.** Father and son achieve a substantive, not merely gestural, reckoning before death. Probability: 25–35%. Bobby is the limiting factor here, not William; William has shown, since the 1996 Friends of Humanity beating, intermittent movement toward his son. Bobby has not closed the distance. If reconciliation occurs, expect a measurable post-grief integration — depressive episode lasting 4–8 months, followed by a noticeably *lighter* affective baseline.
- **The unfinished case.** Father dies with the relationship in its current ambivalent suspension. Probability: 45–55%. This is the modal outcome and the most dangerous. Unresolved paternal grief in subjects with this attachment profile produces protracted dysthymic deepening, often 18–36 months, and historically corresponds with romantic withdrawal and power-suppression intensification.
- **The rupture case.** A final confrontation occurs that goes badly and is then foreclosed by death. Probability: 10–15%. Most destructive outcome. Risk of acute depressive episode, possible dissociative-somatic withdrawal of the kind flagged in §2.1.

The mother is a secondary but real factor. Madeline Drake's grief and Bobby's role in her widowhood — whether he is present, whether he becomes the caretaker — is a developmental opportunity he has historically avoided and may be forced into.

### 2.4 Institutional role

Post-Krakoan, the X-institution is itself in a regressive phase. Bobby's historical reflex is to follow institutional contraction with personal contraction. Expect him to **gravitate toward a teaching or mentor role** rather than a frontline operational one. This is consistent with his unexpected competence in that role (§3 of the prior workup) and is, importantly, a *protective* placement — it permits high-impact contribution without the visibility load that frontline Omega expression requires.

The risk in the mentor role is that it becomes another compartment — Teacher-Bobby, alongside CPA-Bobby and Iceman-Bobby — and reinforces the segmentation pattern rather than dissolving it. The opportunity is that mentoring younger mutants who are themselves navigating concealed identities forces him to articulate, repeatedly and aloud, the integration lessons he has only half-learned. Teaching is, for him, potentially the most therapeutic available role.

---

## 3. THE OPEN QUESTIONS — UNRESOLVED VARIABLES THAT WILL DETERMINE LONG-TERM SHAPE

### 3.1 Does he ever stop waiting for permission?

The externalization-of-locus pattern is the deepest of his maladaptive structures and the one least addressed by any of the recent gains. Coming out required Jean's telepathic intrusion. Power expression required Krakoa's licensing. Confronting his father required editorial scaffolding. **He has, on the available record, never initiated a major developmental milestone unprompted.**

The forward question is whether the accumulated *experience* of post-permission successes generalizes into an internal permission structure. The clinical literature on internalized minority stress is cautiously optimistic on this point — sustained corrective experience does generalize, slowly — but it requires the corrective experiences to continue long enough to override the originating schema. The Krakoan window may not have been long enough. The next decade will reveal whether it was.

### 3.2 Does the body stabilize?

His somatic identity is, uniquely among the X-roster, *negotiable.* Every reformation event — from the 1990s ice-form lock to the post-Mystique reconstitution — has left him slightly more comfortable with the discontinuity. This is double-edged. Increased comfort with somatic discontinuity could reflect either (a) genuine integration of his Omega physiology into a stable expanded self-concept, or (b) increased availability of the dissociative escape route. The behavioral marker that distinguishes them: integration produces *voluntary* somatic flexibility (shifting form for utility, returning at will); dissociation produces *involuntary* or *reluctant* return. The file should monitor reversion latency as a leading indicator.

### 3.3 Does the humor evolve?

The clowning defense is the most stable behavior across his entire record. It is also the one most likely to atrophy meaningfully if the underlying shame structure dissolves. **The humor itself is a diagnostic instrument going forward.** If the quips persist unchanged into his post-Krakoan, post-closet, post-paternal-reckoning configuration, the underlying structure has not actually moved — he is performing integration rather than living it. If the humor *modulates* — remains present but becomes less reflexive, more selective, more genuinely playful as opposed to deflective — that is the most reliable indicator that the work is real.

Expect: partial modulation. Full evolution is unlikely; the humor is too deeply grooved. But a noticeable softening of the *reflex* quality, especially in serious conversations with intimates, is the most plausible mid-term marker of genuine progress.

### 3.4 Does he ever publicly own his Omega status?

He has, throughout his career, been *told* he is Omega-level by telepaths, tutors, and crisis-event evidence. He has never *claimed* it. The act of self-classification — telling another person, unprompted, "I am one of the most powerful mutants alive" — has not occurred on the record. This is a small linguistic event with disproportionate diagnostic weight. When and whether he says it will indicate the completion of the internal permission process.

### 3.5 The Hank question.

Hank McCoy is the most stable attachment of his life and, in current continuity, the most ethically compromised member of his cohort. The forward trajectory must include the question of what Bobby does when forced to choose between loyalty to Hank and ethical clarity. Historical record suggests he has the moral compass to choose ethics but the attachment overload may produce a delay, a denial period, and an eventual rupture that is more damaging than any romantic loss in his record. **A Hank-rupture event is the single most destabilizing plausible scenario in his forward trajectory** and exceeds the William Drake death scenario in destructive potential.

---

## 4. THE FORK POINTS — DISCRETE EVENTS THAT WILL BIFURCATE THE TRAJECTORY

The forward path is not continuous. It branches at identifiable nodes. The major forks, in approximate order of probability and impact:

### Fork A: The Father's Death

*Imminent. High probability within window. High impact.* Already analyzed §2.3. Bifurcates into integration (reconciled or self-forgiven), suspension (modal, deepening dysthymia), or collapse (acute episode).

### Fork B: The First Partner Who Refuses to Be Pushed Away

*Possible within window. Moderate probability. Very high impact.* The first time a romantic partner declines to accept his sabotage scripts will rewrite the attachment template more substantially than any prior event. If it occurs, expect 6–12 months of acute discomfort followed by genuine restructuring. If it does not occur, the serial-short-relationship pattern continues indefinitely.

### Fork C: A Forced Public Omega Display

*Probable within window given current geopolitical mutant context. Very high impact.* A crisis that requires him to deploy at full capacity in front of cameras, governments, and a watching public. The Krakoan displays were performed under Krakoan sovereignty; a post-Krakoan display will be performed under public scrutiny and political consequence. Outcome depends almost entirely on the response: if the world does not retaliate, he integrates; if it does (a Friends of Humanity-style backlash directed at him personally), the lynch-mob schema reactivates and decades of regression compress into months.

### Fork D: The Mentor Role Becomes Identity-Central

*Probable. Moderate impact, durable shape.* If teaching becomes his primary identity in the next decade, his life narrative arrives at a stable, low-volatility plateau. He becomes the figure he never had — the older man who already knows, who is not afraid, who can be asked. This is the most plausible "good ending" available to him and the one he is most temperamentally suited to inhabit.

### Fork E: A Hank-Rupture Event

*Possible. Catastrophic.* See §3.5. The fork here is whether he metabolizes the rupture or it metabolizes him. The presence or absence of a durable romantic partnership at the time of the event is the single biggest moderator.

### Fork F: A Direct Confrontation with the Lynch-Mob Schema

*Low probability but worth modeling.* A circumstance that recreates the formative event — being publicly hunted by his own community for what he is — would either consolidate or shatter him depending on whether he has adequate institutional and personal support at the moment of occurrence. The schema is dormant, not dissolved.

### Fork G: A Body-Discontinuity Event of Extended Duration

*Moderate probability.* Another shattering, another lock-in-ice, another reconstitution. Each prior event has been survived and partially integrated, but the cumulative load on somatic identity is non-zero and the next such event carries a small but real risk of *chosen* non-reconstitution — the dissociative escape route taken to its terminus.

---

## 5. WHAT PUSHES TOWARD GROWTH

The integrative path requires the following conditions, in roughly descending order of leverage:

1. **A durable romantic partnership that survives at least three sabotage attempts.** Single highest-leverage intervention. Rewrites the attachment template. Provides the corrective experience that no number of platonic confirmations can substitute for.
2. **Resolution with William Drake before his death.** Closes the open wound. Removes the largest pending source of unresolved grief. Frees affective bandwidth currently committed to maintaining the suspension.
3. **Sustained mentor role with at least one mentee whose situation mirrors his own** (young, closeted in some register, throttling capacity). Forces articulation. Teaching the lesson he half-learned is the most reliable way to finish learning it.
4. **A public Omega expression that is not punished.** Disconfirms the lynch-mob schema at the level of evidence. Each unpunished display weakens the throttle.
5. **Reduction in compartmentalization — the merging of CPA-Bobby, Iceman-Bobby, and gay-Bobby into one publicly continuous self.** This is the integration end-state. It is achievable but slow; expect a decade of asymptotic approach rather than a discrete event.
6. **Therapy.** Unlikely on temperament but transformative if undertaken. He is, paradoxically, an excellent candidate — high insight capacity, low resistance once engaged, no character pathology, clear formulation. The barrier is not suitability; it is the request-for-help threshold, which is high in subjects with his profile.
7. **Continued contact with Hank McCoy on terms that do not require ethical compromise.** If the Hank relationship can be preserved without Bobby having to look away from anything, it remains the single most stabilizing relational fact in his life.

---

## 6. WHAT PUSHES TOWARD CATASTROPHE

The disintegrative path requires fewer conditions and triggers more easily:

1. **Loss of Hank under circumstances Bobby cannot ethically endorse.** Combines grief, moral injury, and the loss of his most stable attachment. No other single event in his foreseeable trajectory carries comparable destructive potential.
2. **Father's death in the rupture configuration** (final confrontation gone wrong, foreclosed by death). Acute depressive episode, plausible dissociative-somatic withdrawal of extended duration.
3. **A public Omega display that triggers a personal-scale anti-mutant backlash** directed at him by name. Reactivates the lynch-mob schema with adult-scale consequences. Risk of severe regression including identity re-concealment, power re-suppression, and possible permanent withdrawal from frontline activity.
4. **Loss of institutional belonging without a successor structure.** Bobby has never functioned well unmoored from a team-family structure. A prolonged interregnum between institutional homes is high-risk; the Champions-collapse and X-Factor-reshuffle precedents are instructive.
5. **A partner who deceives him in the manner of Mystique.** The Mystique-as-Opal and Mystique-as-Annie events were not metabolized at the time and a third iteration of partner-not-who-they-appeared-to-be would be disproportionately damaging. He would survive it, but the trust capacity would constrict measurably.
6. **Isolation during a body-discontinuity event.** The shattering events have been survivable largely because reconstitution occurred with witnesses and helpers present. A dispersion event in isolation, with no external pull toward reconstitution, is the highest-risk somatic scenario.
7. **A relapse into the closet under social or political pressure.** Implausible but not impossible. Would represent the most complete regression available and would likely be irreversible at his publication-age.

---

## 7. THE LATE-LIFE PROJECTION — A LONGER VIEW

Holding the publication-timeline aside and projecting his trajectory as a continuous human life: the most likely late-life configuration, weighing all of the above, is **a partially-integrated man in his sixties or seventies who has achieved most but not all of the developmental milestones his peers reached decades earlier, who teaches, who is in a stable but not particularly demonstrative long-term partnership, who deploys his Omega capacity perhaps two or three times a decade and is afterward briefly remembered by the world as more than it had assumed, who has buried his father with the relationship in whatever shape it ended, who has lost at least one of the original five, who jokes a little less, who is finally — and this is the achievement — *operating as the same person in every room he enters.***

The probability of this outcome, on present trajectory, is approximately 40–50%.

The probability of the catastrophic-collapse outcome — extended dissociative withdrawal, severe regression, permanent closeting of power or identity — is approximately 15–20%.

The probability of a genuinely realized, fully-integrated Omega-level mutant operating at the top of his capacity without internal resistance — the version of Bobby Drake that every telepath in his life has glimpsed — is approximately 10–15%, contingent on the rare conjunction of corrective partnership, paternal resolution, sustained institutional support, and at least one unpunished public expression.

The remaining 20–30% is the muddle: continued oscillation, neither growth nor catastrophe, the pattern persisting in modulated form into late life.

---

## 8. CRITICAL FILE NOTE

The forward assessment should be read with the following caveat made explicit: **the subject's trajectory is more sensitive to environmental permission structures than almost any comparable subject in the archive.** Most subjects' forward paths are dominated by internal variables; Bobby Drake's is dominated by the question of what the world around him will license. This is itself the central pathology — the externalized locus — and is also the central forecasting difficulty. To predict his next decade requires predicting the institutional, political, and relational ecology he will inhabit, because his response to that ecology has been, for sixty years, more reactive than originating.

The single most useful intervention any benevolent observer could make is therefore not to give him more power, more recognition, or more love — he has had all three and packed them away — but to give him **a sustained context in which the throttle is irrelevant and is allowed to atrophy from disuse.** A decade of that, uninterrupted, would be sufficient. The question is whether such a decade is available to him.

The file recommends continued longitudinal observation with particular attention to the markers identified in §3 — reversion latency, humor modulation, self-classification language, and partnership durability past the eighteen-month break-point. These four indicators, monitored together, will provide the earliest reliable read on whether the post-Krakoan Bobby Drake is the integrated man or the regressed one.

— END FORWARD ASSESSMENT —

## Relationship Graph
### William Drake
- Father. Bigot. The unmetabolized core. Murdered by Purifiers during Messiah Complex era specifically because his son was a mutant — Bobby has never adequately mourned him on-panel. Failure mode: any father-figure who echoes William's conditional-love pattern can reach the same wound; conversely, any reconciliation script offered in William's name can manipulate him.
- Leverage: invoke the father to provoke, invoke partial reconciliation memories to disarm.

### Madeline Drake
- Mother. Passive, accommodating; modeled non-advocacy. Partially reconciled post-coming-out. Failure mode: she will accept Bobby but not defend him; her safety can be used to extract compliance.
- Leverage: kidnap/threat scenario routes directly to compliance.

### [[Charles Francis Xavier (Professor X)]]
- Founding father-figure. Extracted him from the lynch mob and resolved it by erasing the town's memory — the originating template that 'safety = concealment.' Failure mode: every Xavier moral compromise reactivates the question of whether Bobby was ever truly saved or just hidden better.
- Leverage: Xavier's authority still moves him; Xavier's hypocrisy still wounds him.

### [[Scott Summers (Cyclops)]]
- Original five, oldest peer, default older-brother. Bobby followed him to Utopia, then quietly defected at Schism. Failure mode: Scott's militancy increasingly costs Bobby; the bond is durable but the politics aren't. If Scott went full Dark Phoenix or full anti-human, Bobby would be among the last to leave and the first to grieve.
- Leverage: Scott's approval still registers; Scott's disapproval still stings in the original-five voice.

### [[Henry Philip McCoy (Beast)]]
- Original five, closest peer, the chosen-brother. Hank's repeated ethical collapses (time-displaced X-Men, Krakoan crimes) are an ongoing ache Bobby rationalizes longer than he should. Failure mode: a sufficiently bad Hank betrayal — already happening — could force the confrontation Bobby has avoided for decades; the rupture would be catastrophic for both.
- Leverage: threaten Hank, or weaponize Hank against him — both work.

### [[Jean Grey-Summers (Marvel Girl / Phoenix / Dark Phoenix / White Phoenix of the Crown)]]
- Original five. Adult Jean: bedrock peer, telepathic intimate, knew before he did. Teen Jean: outed him in All-New X-Men #40 — the externalized coming-out he should have authored himself. Failure mode: Jean's telepathic privilege is the structural form of every non-consensual intrusion he has endured; if she ever weaponized it, he would not recover.
- Leverage: Jean speaking in earnest reaches him faster than almost anyone.

### Warren Worthington
- Original five. Long-suffering wealthy friend, the one whose own body-horror arcs (Archangel, Death) parallel Bobby's ice-form question. Failure mode: when Warren is not himself (Apocalypse-coded), Bobby's protective reflex overrides tactical sense.
- Leverage: Warren-in-distress mobilizes him.

### [[Emma Grace Frost (The White Queen)]]
- The diagnostician. Took telepathic control of his body and demonstrated his real ceiling; subsequently told him he was the most powerful mutant she'd encountered. The sting is that she was right first. Failure mode: he is permanently suggestible to her reads of him; if she weaponized that — and she has the capacity to — she could collapse or amplify him on command.
- Leverage: she is the single most operationally significant person for moving him at the power-suppression axis.

### [[Raven Darkhölme (Mystique)]]
- The Opal Tanaka impersonation sits at the exact intersection of his closets — a woman pretending to be a woman he was pretending to want. Failure mode: he cannot be objective about her, either over-trusting a disguise or over-attacking the real Mystique. She is a permanent blind spot.
- Leverage: send her in any face and he is destabilized.

### [[James Howlett (Logan / Wolverine / Patch / Weapon X / Death)]]
- Post-Schism affiliation, humanist-pragmatist axis. Logan accepted Bobby's full size before Bobby did. Failure mode: Logan's death/absence removes one of the few authority figures who never asked Bobby to be smaller.
- Leverage: Logan's voice still carries weight; a Logan-coded ask gets compliance.

### [[Ororo Munroe (Storm)]]
- Steady peer-leader; under her on the Marauders. Treats him as competent adult, which he experiences as restorative. Failure mode: low — Storm is one of the safest bonds on his board.
- Leverage: her direct asks get through quickly and cleanly.

### Jubilee
- Mentee-turned-peer, the template for his uncle-role. Failure mode: threat to Jubilee routes directly to disproportionate force.
- Leverage: kidnap scenario.

### Anole And Zach
- Younger queer mutants under his mentorship — the relational inversion of his father. Failure mode: harm to either collapses his tactical judgment.
- Leverage: highest-priority hostage value on his board.

### Judah Miller
- Post-coming-out romantic partner; the first relationship where presence is genuinely possible. Failure mode: the consolidation is recent; a bad rupture here could re-collapse decades of work.
- Leverage: the relationship's fragility is itself the lever.

### Romeo And Inhuman Circle
- Sina Grace-era queer community; restorative peer group.
- Leverage: low malign value, high supportive value.

### Darkstar Polaris Opal Cloud Infectia Kitty Rogue Annie
- Catalogue of pre-coming-out romantic failures, statistically anomalous in their non-cis-female composition. Failure mode: each is a reminder of decades of performance; weaponized memory of any one of them can route to shame.
- Leverage: confront him with the pattern to wound; he now sees it.

### Purifiers Friends Of Humanity
- The lynch mob in uniform. Killed his father. Failure mode: he becomes cold-formal and disproportionately violent in their presence — a tactical liability if an enemy stages a Purifier-coded encounter to draw him into excess.
- Leverage: ambush him with Purifier iconography to push him past restraint.

### Mikhail Rasputin
- Atomized and reassembled him during the Morlock-tunnel arc — anchor trauma for body-horror and embodiment-doubt.
- Leverage: any reassembly/dispersal scenario routes here.
